shared_focus = {
	id = EQS_pony_summit
	icon = GFX_EQS_the_grand_equestria_summit
	x = 12
	y = 0
	cost = 5	
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus EQS_pony_summit"
		add_political_power = 25
		add_stability = 0.05
		country_event = equestria.1
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_STABILITY FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }
}

		else = {
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = armor_bonus
				bonus = 1
				uses = 1
				category = armor
			} 
		}
		set_country_flag = EQS_tempestwind_arrives
		custom_effect_tooltip = EQS_tempestwind_stats_tt

		}

	id = EQS_Equestria_at_war
	available = {
		OR = {
			has_defensive_war = yes
			surrender_progress > 0.05
		}
	}

	y = 11
